	focus = {
		id = BUL_the_great_etatist_project
		icon = GFX_goal_state_economy
		cost = 3

		x = -8
		y = 2
     relative_position_id = BUL_automobile_industry
     prerequisite = {
      focus = BUL_automobile_industry
    }
		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_INDUSTRY }
		ai_will_do = { factor = 50 }
		available = {
			has_war = no
		}
		completion_reward = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus BUL_the_great_etatist_project"
			add_tech_bonus = {
				name = BUL_the_great_etatist_project
				bonus = 1
				uses = 1
				category = industry
			}
			set_variable = { BUL_factory_goals = num_of_factories }
			add_to_variable = { BUL_factory_goals = 10 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_tech = concentrated_industry
						has_tech = dispersed_industry
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = BUL_industry_level_0
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_tech = concentrated_industry
						has_tech = dispersed_industry
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = BUL_industry_level_1
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_tech = concentrated_industry2
						has_tech = dispersed_industry2
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = BUL_industry_level_2
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_tech = concentrated_industry3
						has_tech = dispersed_industry3
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = BUL_industry_level_3
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_tech = concentrated_industry4
						has_tech = dispersed_industry4
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = BUL_industry_level_4
			}
			country_event = bulgariaflavour.4
